### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 38 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two cars are travelling from the same starting point in the same direction, having started their commute at the same time. The first car travels at a steady rate of 55 mph, while the second travels at a steady rate of 52 mph. How much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other?
Choices:
  A: 3 hours
  B: 5 hours
  C: 6 hours
  D: 4 hours
  E: 7 hours
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The relative velocity of the second car, with respect to the first car, is the difference in the velocities.
  The distance between the two cars is increasing at the relative velocity.
  The distance traveled can be calculated by multiplying the rate and the time.
  We can set up a distance equation to solve for the time.
  
Solution:
  Relative velocity = 55 mph - 52 mph = 3 mph
  Let t be the time elapsed for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  Distance = Rate * Time
  15 = 3 * t
  t = 5
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  In relative motion problems, we can add or subtract the velocities of the objects to determine their relative speed.
  We can use the relative speed and the distance to find the time it takes for the objects to reach a certain distance between them.

Solution:
  The relative speed of the second car with respect to the first car is 55 – 52 = 3 mph.
  We want to know the time it takes to travel 15 miles at a speed of 3 mph.
  Time = distance ÷ speed = 15 miles ÷ 3 mph = 5 hours.

Action: Answer("B")

  T = 15 miles / 3 mph
  
  Simplifying the math:

  Solving d - 15 = 52t for d, we find that d = 52t + 15.
  Setting the expressions for d equal to each other, we have 55t = 52t + 15.
  Solving for t, we get t = 5.

Topic: Math
Question: A man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner. He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables. He can only eat one type at a time. In how many ways can he eat breakfast and dinner.
Choices:
  A: 54
  B: 24
  C: 48
  D: 20
  E: 36
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The man wants to eat a fruit for breakfast and a vegetable for dinner.
  He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables.
  The number of options for breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of fruit and the number of vegetables.
Action: Answer("48") 
The number of ways to eat breakfast and dinner is 6 x 8 = 48. Therefore, the answer is C.
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  The man can choose 1 fruit out of 6 for breakfast, and 1 vegetable out of 8 for dinner.
  The number of ways to choose k items out of n items is given by the formula nCk = n! / (k! * (n-k)!), where ! denotes the factorial function that multiplies all positive integers less than or equal to n. The formula counts the ways to choose k items from a set of n items where the order does not matter.
  
Breakfast: choose 1 fruit out of 6.
Dinner: choose 1 vegetable out of 8.
The choices are independent, so the number of ways to choose breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of ways to choose breakfast and the number of ways to choose dinner.

Action: Answer("48")  
The number of ways to choose breakfast is 6C1 = 6.
The number of ways to choose dinner is 8C1 = 8.
The number of ways to choose breakfast and dinner is 6 * 8 = 48.
Response 2:
Knowledge:
To solve the problem, we need to multiply the number of ways that he can eat fruit for breakfast with the number of ways he can eat vegetables for dinner. The two events are independent. Therefore, the total possibilities are their product.

Topic: Math
Question: Suppose for any real number x, [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x. Let L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]. Then it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which
Choices:
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y)
  B: L(x,y) ≠ R(x,y)
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  D: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x.
  L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y]
  R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y) implies [x] + [y] + [x + y] = [2x] + [2y], which is only possible when x and y are integers, but the question does not restrict x and y to be integers.
  B: L(x,y) cannot be equal to R(x,y) for all possible positive real numbers x and y.
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y) means that [x] + [y] + [x + y] < [2x] + [2y]. This is possible if x and y are close enough to integers such that the difference between [x] and x, and the difference between [y] and y are both at most 0.5, and the difference between [x + y] and (x+y) is at most 1. However, for large values of x and y, [2x] and [2y] will be at least twice as big as [x] and [y], making R(x,y) much larger than L(x,y).
  D: L(x,y) > R(x,y) is not possible because [2x] and [2y] can only be larger than or equal to [x] and [y], respectively.
Action: Answer("C")

   [x] + [y] + [x+y] = [2x] + [2y]
   Since the left side is always an integer and the right side is always even integer, 
   [2x] and [2y] both have the same parities as the integer parts of x and y,
   respectively. Therefore, either both are even or both are odd integers.
   On the other hand, [x+y] can be either even or odd integer.
   The only possibility for [x] + [y] + [x+y] = [2x] + [2y] is when
   [x+y] = [2x] + [2y]
   Since [x+y] <= x+y and [2x] <= 2x and [2y] <= 2y,
   [2x] + [2y] <= 2(x+y)
   [x+y] <= [2x] + [2y]

   [x+y] <= x+y < [x+y] + 1/2 and
   [2x] <= 2x < [2x] + 1 and
   [2y] <= 2y < [2y] + 1
   We could try an example, x=1.2, and y=0.3, then
   [x] + [y] + [x+y] = [1] + [0] + [1.5] = 2
   [2x] + [2y] = [2.4] + [0.6] = 3
   Therefore, it is impossible to have L(x,y) = R(x,y).
   So, we only have L(x,y) < R(x,y).
   For example, x=0.2, and y=0.3, then
   [x] + [y] + [x+y] = [0] + [0] + [0.5] = 0
   [2x] + [2y] = [0.4] + [0.6] = 1
   Therefore, it is possible to have L(x,y) < R(x,y).
   Therefore, the answer is (D) L(x,y) < R(x,y).

 Analysis:
  Note that [x+y] ≤ [x] + [y] ≤ [x+y] + 1, since 
  - [x+y] is the largest integer less than or equal to x+y
  - [x] is the largest integer less than or equal to x
  - [y] is the largest integer less than or equal to y
  Therefore, 
  L(x,y) ≤ [x+y] + [x] + [y] + 1 < [x+y] + [2x] + [2y] + 1 ≤ R(x,y) + 1
  Hence, we conclude that L(x,y) cannot equal R(x,y).

  R(x,y) ≤ [2x] + [2y] + 2 < 2[x] + 2[y] + 4 ≤ L(x,y) + 4
  Hence, we conclude that it is also impossible to have L(x,y) < R(x,y).

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 41 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
Choices:
  A: Rs. 697.50
  B: Rs. 712.50
  C: Rs. 787.50
  D: Rs. 750
  E: Rs. 780
Response 0:
Given that the shopkeeper gave a discount of 5% and earned a certain amount of profit while selling the watch. And, if he had given a discount of 7%, he would have earned Rs. 15 lesser. We need to determine the marked price of the watch.

Let's assume the marked price of the watch be M.

When the shopkeeper gave a discount of 5% and earned a certain amount of profit, we can determine that he sold the watch for 95% of its marked price. Thus, his profit would be M*(95/100) - C1, where C1 is the cost price.

Similarly, when the shopkeeper gave a discount of 7% and earned Rs. 15 lesser profit, we can determine that he sold the watch for 93% of its marked price. Thus, his profit would be M*(93/100)-15 - C2, where C2 is the cost price.

We can equate the two expressions for the profit and solve for the marked price M.

M*(95/100) - C1 = M*(93/100) - 15 - C2

M*(2/100) = C1 - C2 + 15

M = (C1-C2+15)*50

Now, we do not have exact values of C1 and C2. But we can determine their difference from the given information. 

We know that giving a discount of 5%, the shopkeeper earned some profit. And, if he had given the discount of 7%, he would earn Rs. 15 lesser as profit. This means that the difference between the two profits should be Rs. 15. And the percentage difference in profit can be calculated by taking the ratio of the difference in profit to the profit at 5% discount.

Profit percentage difference = [ (M*(93/100)-15 - C2) - (M*(95/100) - C1) ] / (M*(95/100) - C1) * 100

Simplifying, we get:

Profit percentage difference = 100*(2*C1 - 3*C2 + 30) / (95*C1 - 93*C2)

Now, for some values of C1 and C2, this fraction should be equal to 2.5% (given that the difference in profit is Rs. 15 and we need to convert the difference to percentage), which is equal to 0.025 when expressed as a decimal. 

We can try different values of C1 and C2 to find a pair of values that satisfy the equation. 

Let's assume that the cost price, C1 = Rs. 100.
Then we can solve for C2 using the information that the profit percentage difference is 2.5%.

C2 = (2*C1 + 30 - 0.025*95*C1) / 3

C2 = Rs. 77.50

Substituting C1 and C2 in the expression we derived for the marked price M, we get:

M = (C1-C2+15)*50

M = Rs. 712.50

Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 712.50

Answer: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
Let the marked price of the watch be M.
Let the cost price of the watch be C.
The shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, so the selling price is 0.95*M.
If he gives a discount of 7%, then the selling price is 0.93*M.
If he gives a discount of 7%, then the profit earned is M - C - 0.93*M = 0.07*M - C.
Since the shopkeeper earns Rs. 15 less as profit, we have 0.07*M - C = 0.07*M - C + 15, which simplifies to C = 15.
Action: Answer("D") 
Using this information in the formula for profit above, we have:
M - C - 0.95*M = M - C - 0.93*M + 15
Simplifying this equation gives M = 750. Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.
Response 2:
Let the marked price of the watch be x.

If the shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, he sells the watch for 0.95x.
If the shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, he sells the watch for 0.93x.

According to the problem, by giving a 7% discount instead of a 5% discount, the shopkeeper earns Rs. 15 less as profit. This means that the difference in profit between the 5% discount and 7% discount is Rs. 15.

We can write an equation to represent the above information:

0.05x = 0.07x + 15

Simplifying the equation, we get:

-0.02x = 15

x = -15/(-0.02)

x = 750

Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.

  The profit (P1) made by the shopkeeper in the first transaction = 0.95 * MP - x.

  -0.02 * MP = 15 - 0.02 * x
  MP = (15 - 0.02 * x)/(-0.02)

  Solving the above equation, we get:
  MP = 750

Topic: Math
Question: I have a money pouch containing Rs. 700. There are equal number of 25 paise coins, 50 paise coins and one rupee coins.

Choices:
  A: 453

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 43 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The height of a room to its semi-perimeter is 2:5. It costs Rs.260 to paper the walls of the room with paper 50cm wide at Rs.2 per meter allowing an area of 15 sq.m for doors and windows. The height of the room is:
Choices:
  A: 2.6m
  B: 3.9m
  C: 4m
  D: 4.2m
  E: 4.4m
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Semiperimeter of a room is the sum of the lengths of all its sides divided by 2.
  We can use ratios to find a relationship between the height of the room and the lengths of its sides.
  We can use the cost and area information to find the dimensions of the room.

Action: Answer("D") - 4.2m

Solution:
  Let h be the height of the room and p be its semiperimeter.
  From the problem, we have h:p/2 = 2:5, which simplifies to h = 2p/5.
  Let l be the length of the room and w be the width.
  Then, p = l + w + l + w = 2l + 2w, so p/2 = l + w.
  Substituting h = 2p/5, we have h = 4(l + w)/5.
  The area of the four walls of the room is (l + w)h, which is equal to (5/4)hp.
  Let A be the area of the walls that need to be covered with paper, and let a be the width of the doors and windows.
  Then, A = (5/4)hp - 15 and a = 15/w.
  The cost of the paper is Rs.260, which is equal to the length of the walls that need to be covered with paper times the cost per unit length.
  Let c be the cost per unit length of the paper.
  Then, 260 = (l + w)A/c = (2l + 2w)(4h/5)((5/4)hp - 15)/c.
  Simplifying, we have 104 = 8lw(hp - 3a)/5c.
  Substituting h = 4p/5 and a = 15/w, we have 104 = 96lw(p^2/5c - 9/w).
  Solving for lw, we have lw = 5c/24(p^2/w^2 - 9).
  Since the width of the paper is 50cm, which is 0.5m, the length of the paper needed is l + w + l + w + a + a = 2l + 4w + 30/w.
  Substituting h = 4p/5 and A = (5/4)hp - 15, we have A/w = (2h - 6/w)(l + w) = (8p/5 - 6/w)(2l + 2w).
  Multiplying out and simplifying, we have (p^2/w - 18)/5 = (l + w)(8p/5 - 6/w).
  Substituting lw = 5c/24(p^2/w^2 - 9) and solving for l + w, we have l + w = 5c/6(p/w - 3/w^2).
  Substituting l + w = (2/5)h(p/2) and h = 4p/5, we have p = 25sqrt(c)/(6sqrt(2)).
  Substituting p = 2l + 2w, we have lw = (25c/96)(2/sqrt(2))^2/w^2 = (25c/48)(p^2/w^4 - 1).
  Substituting lw = 5c/24(p^2/w^2 - 9) and solving for w^2, we have w^4 - (9c/5)p^2w^2 - 36c/25 = 0.
  Using the quadratic formula, we get w^2 = (9c/10)p^2 ± sqrt((81c^2/100)p^4 + 144c^2/25)/2.
  Since w^2 > 0, we have p^2 > 1600c/27 and w^2 = (9c/10)p^2 + sqrt((81c^2/100)p^4 + 144c^2/25)/2.
  Substituting p = 25sqrt(c)/(6sqrt(2)), we have w^2 = (25c/72)sqrt(2) + sqrt(625c^2/24).
  Therefore, w^2 = 25c(6 + 2sqrt(2))/36.
  Substituting h = 4p/5 and w^2 = 25c(6 + 2sqrt(2))/36, we have h = p(6 + 2sqrt(2))/9sqrt(5) = 4.2m (approx).
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
The height of the room to its semi-perimeter being 2:5 implies that the height of the room is 2x and its semi-perimeter is 5x.
We know that the cost of the wallpaper is Rs.2 per linear meter and the width of the wallpaper is 50cm or 0.5m. Thus, the cost of wallpaper per square meter is Rs.4.
The area of the walls to be papered is (semi-perimeter x height - area of doors and windows).
We can use the values obtained above to form a quadratic equation which we can solve to find the value of x and then calculate the height of the room.

Action: Answer("C") 
(The height of the room is 4m)
Response 2:
Knowledge:
  Semi-perimeter is (perimeter of the room) / 2.
  Wallpaper costs Rs.2 per meter and it is 50cm wide, which is 0.5m wide.
  The area of the doors and windows is given as 15 sq.m.

Let H be the height of the room, and S be the semi-perimeter.
From the given information, we have:
  H:S = 2:5
  Cost of wallpaper = Rs.260
  Cost per meter of wallpaper = Rs.2
  Width of wallpaper = 50cm = 0.5m
  Area of doors and windows = 15 sq.m

Let's solve for the height of the room now.
  
  Let 5x be the perimeter of the room.
  Then, we have 2x as the height of the room.
  Semi-perimeter, S = (5x)/2

  Let's calculate the area of four walls of the room.
  Length of each wall = Height of the room = 2x
  Total wall area = 2*(height + length)*S = 2*(2x + 5x)*S = 14xS

  Let A be the area to be covered by the wallpaper.
  A = Total wall area - Area of doors and windows
  A = 14xS - 15

  Total cost of wallpaper = Cost per meter * Length of wallpaper required
  Length of wallpaper required = Total area to be covered / Width of one roll of wallpaper  
                              = A / 0.5 = 2A

  Total cost of wallpaper = 2A * 2 = 4A
  4A = 260
  A = 65

  We need to find the height of the room, 2x, where S = (5x)/2
  A = 14xS - 15
  65 = 14x(5x/2) - 15
  65 = 35x^2 - 15
  35x^2 = 80
  x^2 = 80/35
  x = sqrt(8/7)

  Height of the room = 2x = 2*2x/2 = 2*sqrt(8/7) = 4*sqrt(2/7)

Response 3:
Knowledge:
  1. The semi-perimeter of a room is half the sum of all the room's sides.
  2. The height of a room is the distance between the ceiling and the floor.
  3. The cost of papering the walls of a room is dependent on the dimensions of the room and the cost of paper per meter.
  4. To calculate the area of a rectangle, we can multiply the length and width of the rectangle.
  
Solution:
Let 2x be the height of the room and 5x be the semi-perimeter of the room.
The perimeter of the room equals 2 * semi-perimeter = 2 * 5x = 10x
We know that the width of the paper is 50 cm = 0.5 m and the cost of 1 m of paper is Rs. 2. Therefore, the cost of covering 1 sq.m with paper is Rs. 4. 

Let the length, width, and height of the room be L, B, and H, respectively.
Then, we have (L*H + B*H - 15) * 4 = 260.
Simplifying the equation gives us L*H + B*H = 68.
Since the area of the room is LBH, we have LBH = L*H + B*H + 2LB = 68 + 2LB. 

Substituting L = 2*semi-perimeter - H = 10x - 2x = 8x and B = semi-perimeter - H = 5x - 2x = 3x, we get:
8x * 2x * 3x = 68 + 2(8x*3x)
48x^3=68+48x^2
4x^3=17+3x^2
We know that the height (H) is 2x. Thus, the height of the room is:
H = 2x = 2(17/4)^0.5 or approximately 2.6m.

  So, (l + 2y) = 28 and h = 2lx

  l^2 + (2lx)^2 = (5y)^2, where y = (l+2y)/5 = 28/5
  l^2 + 4l^2(x^2) = 25(l+2y)^2/25 = 25(28^2)/25
  l^2(4x^2+1) = 28^2*25 - 4*25l^2
  l^2(4x^2+1) = 25(4*28^2 - l^2)
  
  After some calculation, we get l^2 = 400, then l = 20, x = 5, and h = 2lx = 10x = 50

Topic: Math
Question: A man walks at 5 kmph for 6 hrs and at 4 kmph for 12 hrs. His average speed is
Choices:
  A: 4 1/3 km/h
  B: 7 2/3 km/h
  C: 9 ½ km/h
  D: 8 km/h
  E: 81 km/h
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Average speed is defined as total distance covered divided by total time taken.
  We can use the formula, distance = speed x time, to find the distance traveled at each speed.
  We can then find the total distance traveled and total time taken, and divide to find the average speed.
Calculation:
  Distance traveled at 5 kmph in 6 hours = 5 x 6 = 30 km.
  Distance traveled at 4 kmph in 12 hours = 4 x 12 = 48 km.
  Total distance traveled = 30 + 48 = 78 km.
  Total time taken = 6 + 12 = 18 hours.
  Average speed = total distance traveled / total time taken
                = 78 / 18
                = 13 / 3
                = 4 1/3 km/h (approx)
Action: Answer("A")

Choices:

Question: The difference between the squares of two numbers is 256000 and the sum of the numbers is 1000. The numbers are
Choices:
  A: 600, 400
  B: 628, 372
  C: 640, 360
  D: None of these
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let x and y be the two numbers
  The problem can be translated to the following system of equations:
    x + y = 1000
    x^2 - y^2 = 256000
  We can solve this system of equations to find the values of x and y.

Calculations:
  From the first equation, y = 1000 - x
  Substituting y by its value in the second equation, we get:
    x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
  Solving for x, we get:
    x = 628 or x = 372
  If x = 628, then y = 1000 - 628 = 372
  If x = 372, then y = 1000 - 372 = 628
  Therefore, the numbers are 628 and 372.

Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  Let the two numbers be x and y. Then we have the system of equations:
    x + y = 1000
    x^2 - y^2 = 256000
  Solving the first equation for y, we get y = 1000 - x. Substituting this into the second equation and simplifying, we get:
    x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
    2000x - 1000000 = 256000
    2000x = 1256000
    x = 628
  Substituting this value of x into the equation y = 1000 - x, we get y = 372.
  Therefore, the two numbers are 628 and 372.
Action: Answer("B")

x^2 - y^2 = 256000

x + y = 1000

We can solve for y in terms of x from the second equation:
y = 1000 - x

x^2 - (1000-x)^2 = 256000

-2000x + 1000000 = 256000

x = 628 or x = 372

If x is 628, then y is 372, which satisfies both equations.
If x is 372, then y is 628, which also satisfies both equations.

Therefore, the numbers are 628 and 372.

  Substituting the second equation into the first equation: 
    (x + y)(x - y) = 256000
    x - y = 256000/(x + y)
  We can add the two equations to get 2x = 1000 + 256000/(x + y), which we can solve for x and then find y.

    2x = 1000 + 256000/(x + y)

    x - y = 256000/(x + y)

Calculation:

We can try partitioning 512 into two factors whose difference is a multiple of 2 with the values very close to but smaller than 500.
    512 can be partitioned as (256, 2) and (128, 4) → none of these work. 
    512 can be partitioned as (512, 1) and (64, 8) → none of these work.
    512 can be partitioned as (32, 16) and (32, -16) → (x, y) = (512+32, 500-16) = (544, 484).
    (x-y)(x+y) = (544-484)(544+484) = 60*1028 = 256000
  Therefore, the answer is (x, y) = (544, 484).

Topic: Math
Question: A company produces 420 units of a particular computer component every month, at a production cost to the company of $110 per component, and sells all of the components by the end of each month. What is the minimum selling price per component that will guarantee that the yearly profit (revenue from sales minus production costs) will be at least $626,400 ?
Choices:
  A: 226
  B: 230
  C: 240
  D: 260
  E: 280
Response 0:
Knowledge:
- The company produces 420 components every month, so the annual production is 420*12=5040 components.
- The production cost of each component is $110.
- The profit is the difference between the revenue and the cost.
- The minimum selling price per component can be calculated based on the minimum revenue required.

Calculation:
- The production cost of 5040 components is 5040*$110=$554,400.
- To achieve a yearly profit of $626,400, the total revenue from selling the components should be $626,400+$554,400=$1,180,800.
- The minimum selling price per component to achieve this revenue is $1,180,800/5040=$234.
- The only option close to this value is option B: 230.

Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Let's breakdown the given information to acquire a better understanding:
- We have monthly production, so we need to calculate the monthly profit first.
- We are selling all components produced, so there is no money or waste.
- Monthly profit = Monthly revenue - Monthly production costs = (Monthly selling price * Units produced) - (Monthly production cost * Units produced)
- Yearly profit = Monthly profit * 12 (since there are 12 months a year)
To calculate the minimum selling price, we need to calculate the Monthly selling price that would yield Yearly profit >= $626,400.
Therefore, monthly profit >= 52,200 ($626,400/12)

Calculation:
- Monthly revenue = Units produced * Monthly selling price
- Monthly profit = Monthly revenue - Monthly production costs
- 420x* - 420(110) >= 52,200
- 420x >= 96,600
- x >= 230 ($ rounded to the above integer)

Question: If m > 0, y > 0, and x is m percent of 4y, then, in terms of y, m is what percentage of x?
Choices:
  A: y/400
  B: 4y
  C: 50y
  D: 2500/y
  E: 5000/y
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If x is m percent of y, then x = (m/100)y
  x is m percent of 4y, then x = (m/100)(4y) = (4m/100)y = (m/25)y
  
To convert this equation into m as a percentage of x:
  m = (x/y)*100
  m = (1/[(y/x)/100]) = (1/[(25/m)/100]) = 4m
Therefore, m is 4 percent of x.

Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
(Note: None of the above choices represent 4 percent, which is the correct answer)
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  1. To convert a percent to a decimal, we divide by 100.
  2. To convert a decimal to a percent, we multiply by 100.
  3. If x is m percent of y, then x = (m/100) * y.
  
Let P be the percentage that m is of x.
Then we have: 

    P% = (m/x) * 100%
    
Substituting x = 4y * (m/100), we get:

    P% = m / (4y * (m/100)) * 100%
       = (m/m) * (100/4) * 100%
       = 2500/m %
       
Therefore, the answer is D: 2500/y.
Response 2:

           x = m/100 * 4y

  We can now write m in terms of x:
           m = 25x/y
  And m as a percentage of x:
           m/x = (25x/y) / x
                   = 25/y
  Expressing 25/y as a percentage of x:
           (25/y) / x * 100% = 2500/y %

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 50 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A starts travel towards south 3km, then travel 5 km towards east, and again travels 3 km to north, and finally travels 2km towards west. In the end how far from is A from home?
Choices:
  A: 3km
  B: 2km
  C: 4km
  D: 5km
  E: 6km
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  This is a question about finding the displacement of a person traveling along different directions - north, south, east, or west.
  Displacement refers to the overall change of position of the person with respect to the starting point (which is the home here).
  In geometrical terms, magnitude of displacement can be calculated using the Pythagorean theorem.
  Total distance traveled is not relevant to the calculation of this problem.
Calculation:
  Distance traveled towards south = 3 km (opposite direction to north)
  Distance traveled towards east = 5 km (opposite direction to west)
  Distance traveled towards north = 3 km
  Distance traveled towards west = 2 km
  Adding distance covered towards south and north = 3 km - 3 km = 0 km
  Adding distance covered towards east and west = 5 km - 2 km = 3 km
  Therefore, the overall displacement (distance from home) = square root of (0^2 + 3^2) km = 3 km
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  The net displacement is the shortest distance and straight line from starting point to finishing point.
  Applying Pythagoras theorem to calculate net displacement from distance traveled in x and y direction.
  A: The shortest distance from starting point is not 3 km towards south.
  B: The shortest distance from starting point is not 2 km towards west.
  C: The net displacement can be calculated as (3^2+ (5-2)^2)^0.5 = (9+9)^0.5 = 3(2)^0.5 km.
  D: The shortest distance from starting point is not 5 km towards east.
  E: The shortest distance from starting point is not 6 km towards north.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Knowledge:
  We need to find the resultant distance and displacement of A.
  Displacement is the straight-line distance between the starting and ending point of A's journey.
  Resultant distance is the actual ground path traveled by A.
  The Pythagorean theorem can be used to find the displacement of A.
  We can get the resultant distance by adding all the individual distances travelled by A.

Action: Answer("C") 

To solve this problem, we can draw A's path on a graph. We know that A travelled 3 km south, 5 km east, 3 km north, and 2 km west. We can then create a right triangle with legs of length 3 km and 2 km, and use the Pythagorean theorem to find the displacement of A, which is the hypotenuse of the right triangle.

Using the Pythagorean theorem, the displacement of A works out to be:
displacement = sqrt(3^2 + 2^2)
              = sqrt(9 + 4)
              = sqrt(13) km

The resultant distance travelled by A is:
resultant distance = 3 + 5 + 3 + 2
                   = 13 km

Therefore, A is 4 km away from home.
Response 3:
Knowledge: The final position of A can be found using the pythagorean theorem, where the hypotenuse is the distance from A to home.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 4:
Knowledge:
  This question requires finding the net displacement of the person from their starting point. 
  To solve this problem, we will need to find the horizontal and vertical displacements separately and then combine them to find the net displacement using the Pythagorean theorem.
  Displacement is a vector quantity, which means it has both magnitude (distance) and direction, and it can be represented by an arrow.
  In this question, the direction of North is opposite to South and the direction of West is opposite to East.

Working:
  A starts travel towards south 3km = 3 km South
  Then travel 5 km towards east = 5 km East
  Again travels 3 km to north = 3 km North
  Finally travels 2 km towards west = 2 km West
  We can represent this information as displacement vectors: 3 km South (-3 km, 0 km); 5 km East (0 km, 5 km); 3 km North (3 km, 5 km); and 2 km West (3 km, 3 km)

  To find the net displacement, we need to add the horizontal and vertical components of the displacement vectors algebraically:
  Horizontal displacement = -3 km + 3 km + 0 km - 2 km = -2 km (West)
  Vertical displacement = 0 km + 5 km + 3 km + 0 km = 8 km (North)
  Net displacement = sqrt( (-2 km)^2 + (8 km)^2 ) = sqrt( 4 + 64) = 8.246 km (rounded to three decimal places)

Action: Answer("E")
Response 5:
Knowledge: 
  If someone travels towards South then towards East and then towards North and then towards West, then they end up at the starting point.
  Therefore, the distance of A from Home will be the distance from his starting point to the end point of his travel.
  Let's say A starts from point X.
  After traveling 3 km towards South, A will end up at point Y, which is 3 km South of X.
  After traveling 5 km towards East from point Y, A will end up at point Z, which is 5 km East of Y and 3 km South of X.
  After traveling 3 km towards North from point Z, A will end up at point W, which is 3 km North of Z, 5 km East of Y and 3 km South of X.
  After traveling 2 km towards West from point W, A will end up at point P, which is 2 km West of W, 3 km North of Z, 5 km East of Y and 3 km South of X. 
  To find the distance of AP, we can apply the Pythagoras theorem on right-angled triangle APW.
  Pythagoras theorem: In a right-angled triangle, the square of the hypotenuse is equal to the sum of the squares of the other two sides.
  Therefore, AP = sqrt(PW^2 + AW^2)
  We can calculate PW as 2 km (given in the question).
  To calculate AW, we can add the vertical distances (North-South distances) and the horizontal distances (East-West distances) separately.
  North-South distance = 3 km (from X to Y) - 3 km (from Z to W) = 0 km
  East-West distance = 5 km (from Y to Z) + 2 km (from W to P) = 7 km
  Therefore, AW is 7 km.
  AP = sqrt(PW^2 + AW^2) = sqrt(2^2 + 7^2) = sqrt(53) km.

Therefore, A is sqrt(29) km away from home, which is approximately 5.385 km.

Topic: Math
Question: What should come in place of the question mark(?) in each of the following questions ?
a2 - b2/(a + b)2 (?)=(a - b)2
Choices:
  A: (a + b)(a - b)
  B: (a - b)2
  C: (a + b)2
  D: a3 + b3
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
We can factorize a^2 - b^2 as (a+b)(a-b). 
(a+b)² = a² + 2ab + b²
(a-b)² = a² - 2ab + b²
Using these identities, we can simplify the left-hand side of the given equation as:
a^2 - b^2 / (a+b)^2 = (a+b)(a-b) / (a+b)(a+b)
                        = (a-b)/(a+b)

Now we can substitue this value in place of the question mark and simplify the resulting expression as follows:
(a-b)/(a+b) = (a-b)² / (a+b)²
                     = (a² - 2ab + b²) / (a² + 2ab + b²)
                     = [(a-b)² + 4ab] / [(a+b)²]

So the answer is (C) (a + b)². 

Action: Answer("C")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 52 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: M = abc is a three digit number and N = cba, if M > N and M - N + 396c = 990. Then how many values of M are more than 300.
Choices:
  A: 20
  B: 30
  C: 40
  D: 200
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  The condition that M > N can be expressed as a > c and 100a + 10b + c > 100c + 10b + a.
  This simplifies to 99a > 99c which means a > c.
  From the given equation M - N + 396c = 990, we can substitute M = 100a + 10b + c and N = 100c + 10b + a. This yields:
  (100a + 10b + c) - (100c + 10b + a) + 396c = 990, which simplifies to
  99a - 99c + 396c = 990, which simplifies to
  99a + 297c = 990, which simplifies to 
  a + 3c = 10.

Action: Answer("B") 

Next, we need to find the values of M that are greater than 300 and satisfy the above conditions.
Since a > c, the only possible values of (a, c) that satisfy a + 3c = 10 and have a > c are (4, 2) and (5, 1).
For (a, c) = (4, 2), there are 4 choices for b (namely 0, 1, 3, and 4).
For (a, c) = (5, 1), there are 5 choices for b (namely 0, 2, 3, 4, and 5).
Thus, the total number of values of M that are more than 300 is 2 x (4 + 5) = 18, which is closest to option B, 30.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  - The numbers M and N are formed by the digits of the three-digit integer abc and cba, respectively, where a, b, and c are single-digit integers.
  - We know that M is greater than N. Since a, b, and c are digits of a three-digit integer, we know that none of them can be 0.
  - M = abc = 100a + 10b + c, N = cba = 100c + 10b + a, M - N = 99(a-c) > 0, so a > c.
  - We are given that M - N + 396c = 990.
  - We need to find how many values of M are more than 300. 

Solution: 
  We know that M = abc > 300, which means a = 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, or 9.
  We also know that M - N = 99(a-c), so a-c > 0, which means c < a.
  Since a and c are both digits, there are only a few possible pairs of a and c that satisfy a > c. These pairs are:
  (a, c) = (4, 1), (5, 1), (6, 1), (7, 1), (5, 2), (6, 2), (7, 2), (6, 3), (7, 3), (7, 4)
  We can calculate the corresponding values of M for each of these pairs of a and c using M = 100a + 10b + c, where b can be any digit from 0 to 9. We can then count the number of these values of M that are greater than 300. 
  The values of M for each pair of a and c are:
  - (4, 1): M = 401, 402, ..., 409 (9 values)
  - (5, 1): M = 501, 502, ..., 509 (9 values)
  - (6, 1): M = 601, 602, ..., 609 (9 values)
  - (7, 1): M = 701, 702, ..., 709 (9 values)
  - (5, 2): M = 521, 522, ..., 529 (8 values)
  - (6, 2): M = 621, 622, ..., 629 (8 values)
  - (7, 2): M = 721, 722, ..., 729 (8 values)
  - (6, 3): M = 631, 632, ..., 639 (8 values)
  - (7, 3): M = 731, 732, ..., 739 (8 values)
  - (7, 4): M = 741, 742, ..., 749 (8 values)
  Total number of values of M greater than 300 is: 9+9+9+9+8+8+8+8+8+8 = 84.
  Therefore, the answer is 84, which corresponds to choice C.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Let's start by writing out the values for M and N:
- M = 100a + 10b + c
- N = 100c + 10b + a

We know that M > N, which means that 100a + 10b + c > 100c + 10b + a. Simplifying this gives us:
99a > 99c
a > c

Since M is a three-digit number and a > c, we know that a is either 2 or 3.

Now let's look at the equation M - N + 396c = 990. We can substitute in the expressions for M and N that we wrote earlier to get:
100a + 10b + c - (100c + 10b + a) + 396c = 990

Simplifying this equation gives us:
99a + 295c = 990

We know that a is either 2 or 3, so let's try both cases:

If a = 2:
99(2) + 295c = 990
295c = 792
c = 792/295, which is not an integer. So a cannot be 2.

If a = 3:
99(3) + 295c = 990
295c = 693
c = 693/295, which is also not an integer. So a cannot be 3.

Therefore, there are no values of M that satisfy the given conditions.

Choices:

  B: 240
  C: 30
  D: 60
  E: 120
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Distance = Speed x Time (D = S x T)
  We are given the Speed (S) which is 12 mph.
  We are required to find time in minutes which means we should convert the speed (S) to miles per minute.
  
Calculation:
  Speed in miles per minute = Speed in miles per hour / 60 (because 1 hour = 60 minutes)
  Speed in miles per minute = 12 / 60
  Speed in miles per minute = 0.2 miles per minute
  
  We know that distance (D) is 48 miles.
  D = S x T
  48 = 0.2 x T
  T = 48 / 0.2
  T = 240 minutes

  Time = 4 hours

  Time in minutes = 240

Question: Everyone in the family earns money each month. If the total income of a family per month is $9000 and the median income is $3000, how many members are there in the family?
Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Median is the value separating the higher half from the lower half of a sample. 
  If we arrange the incomes for each member in ascending order, the median will be the income of the middle member.
  Let's assume there are "n" members in the family. 
  We know that the total income (TI) of the family is $9000 and the median income (MI) is $3000.
 
  If we arrange the incomes in ascending order, the median income will be the income of the (n+1)/2 member (if "n" is odd) or the average between the incomes of the 2 central members:
 
    MI = (X[n/2] + X[n/2 + 1])/2 (if n is even)
 
  Also, we know that the total income (TI) is simply the sum of each member's income:
 
    TI = X[1] + X[2] + ... + X[n]
 
  We can use these equations to solve for the value of "n".

  Action: Answer("3")

  The total income of a family is the sum of incomes of its members.
  If the median income is $3000, we know that at least one member earns exactly $3000. 

Calculation:

  There are also x family members earning more than $3000.

Response 6:

  * The median income is $3000, which means that at least half of the family members earn that amount.

Calculation:
  * We know that the median income is the income of some middle member of the family.
  * Since half of the family members earn the same or less than the median, and the total income is $9000 per month, the sum of their incomes is at least $9000 / 2 = $4500.
  * For the median to be exactly $3000, there must be at least one family member who earns exactly $3000, and the total sum of incomes for all family members who earn less than $3000 is $4500 - $3000 = $1500.
  * The number of family members who earn less than $3000 is then $1500 / $2000 = 0.75 members, which means that it must be at least 1, and at most 2 members.
  * To get the total number of family members, we need to add the number of members who earn $3000 or more. Half of the family members earn $3000 or above, so their total income is at least $4500, which is the rest of the family's income that we haven't accounted for yet. 
  * The number of members who earn that amount or more is then $4500 / $3000 = 1.5 members, which means it must be at least 1, and at most 2 members.
  * Therefore, there are either 2 or 4 members in the family.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 55 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A starts a business with Rs.40,000. After 2 months, B joined him with Rs.60,000. C joined them after some more time with Rs.120,000. At the end of the year, out of a total profit of Rs.375,000, C gets Rs.150,000 as his share. How many months after B joined the business, did C join?
Choices:
  A: 2 months
  B: 4 months
  C: 23 months
  D: 24 months
  E: 84 months
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  We know that A and B started the business together and afterwards C joined the business.
  We also know that C's profit is Rs.150,000 and total profit is Rs.375,000.
  We are also given the initial investments of A, B and C and time period of A and B (which is 12-2=10 months).
  We can solve the problem using the concept of ratio and proportion. 

Step 1: Find the ratio of profit sharing among A, B and C
  Here, C gets Rs.150,000 out of the total profit of Rs.375,000
  So, the ratio of C's profit sharing = 150000/375000 = 2/5
  Let the ratio of profit sharing among A, B and C be a:b:c
  Then, a:b:c = x:y:2/5
  where x and y are ratios for A and B respectively.
  
Step 2: Find the ratio of investment and time period for A, B and C
  A invested Rs.40,000 for 12 months = 40,000*12 = 480,000
  B invested Rs.60,000 for 10 months (after 2 months of A's investment) = 60,000*10 = 600,000
  Let C invested Rs.z for t months
  Then, (480000):(600000):(z*t) = (2y):(3y):(2t/y)
  Simplifying this equation, we get:
  16z = 5yt
  
Step 3: Find the time period for C
  We are given C's investment as Rs.120,000.
  From step 2, we know that 16z = 5yt
  Substituting the values we have, we get:
  16*120000 = 5y*t
  1920000 = 5y*t
  t = 1920000/5y
  
Step 4: Substitute t in the equation for profit sharing ratios
  a:b:c = x:y:2/5
  but we need to calculate x:y
  Total investment by A and B = 480000 + 600000 = 1080000
  C's investment = 120000
  So, (a+b):c = 1080000:120000 = 9:1
  Also, (a/b) = (2/5)/(1-(2/5)) = 2/3
  Therefore, (9y/3):(y/3) = 9:1
  So, x:y = 8:1
  
Step 5: Find the answer
  From step 3, we know that t = 1920000/5y
  Also, from step 4, we know that x:y = 8:1
  Therefore, (a/(a+b)) = y/(x+y) = 1/9
  A worked for 10 months, so (a/(a+b)) = 10/12 = 5/6
  Therefore, (y/(x+y)) = (1/9)*(6/5) = 2/15
  
  Let z be the time period for C in months.
  Then, (z/(10+z)) = (2/15)
  Solving this equation, we get:
  z = (150/7) months 
  
Action: Answer("C")  - 23 months (approx)
Response 1:
Let's work through this problem step by step:
Let x be the time (in months) after B joined the business that C joined.
A invested 40000 for 12 months. Therefore, his investment = 40000 * 12 = Rs. 480000
B invested 60000 for 10 months. Therefore, his investment = 60000 * 10 = Rs. 600000
C invested 120000 for (10-x) months. Therefore, his investment = 120000 * (10-x) = Rs. 1200000 - 120000x
Their total investment = Rs. 480000 + Rs. 600000 + Rs. (1200000 - 120000x) = Rs. (2280000 - 120000x)
C's profit share = Rs. 150000
Total profit = Rs. 375000
C's profit share / Total profit = (1200000 - 120000x) / (2280000 - 120000x) = 150000 / 375000 = 2/5
Solving the above equation, we get x = 4 months
Therefore, C joined 4 months after B joined the business.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Let's first determine A and B's total investment while C was not yet part of the business:
A invested for the whole year so his investment is 40000*12 = 480000
B invested for only 10 months (since he joined after 2 months) so his investment is 60000*10 = 600000
Total investment for A and B = 480000 + 600000 = 1080000

Let's then determine C's investment:
Since A and B already had a total investment of Rs. 1080000 when C joined, all of C's Rs. 120000 is only a fraction of the total investment he is part of:
Let x be the number of months after B joined that C joined.
Total investment after B joined but before C joined is:
A's investment + B's investment = 40000*2 + 60000*x = 80000 + 60000x
Total investment after C joined is:
Total investment after B joined but before C joined + C's investment = 120000 + 80000 + 60000x = 200000 + 60000x

The business earned a total profit of Rs. 375000 and C's share in that profit is Rs. 150000, so the remaining profit is Rs. 225000 which is divided between A and B. Since we know their investment and the length of time they invested, we can calculate how much each should get. In particular, we should have:
C's share / Remaining profit = C's investment / Total investment
which we can solve for x.

We get:
150000 / 225000 = 120000 / (200000 + 60000x)
=> 4 / 6 = 3 / (5 + x)
=> x = 23

Therefore, C joined 23 months after B.

- Solving for x: 1000 = 0.05x, x = 20,000
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The shop assistant's salary is composed of a fixed salary of $500 and a commission of 5% of the monthly sales.
  We need to find out how much the monthly sales should be so that her salary reaches $1500.
  Let's call the monthly sales x.
  Her monthly salary S can be calculated using the equation S = $500 + 0.05x

Calculation:
  We need to solve the equation S = $1500 by substituting S = $500 + 0.05x
  $500 + 0.05x = $1500
  0.05x = $1500 - $500
  0.05x = $1000
  x = $1000/0.05
  x = $20000

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 57 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The sum of k consecutive integers is 51. If the least integer is -50, then k =
Choices:
  A: 40
  B: 62
  C: 82
  D: 92
  E: 102
Response 0:
Let n be the first integer of the k consecutive integers. We can set up an equation:
n + (n+1) + (n+2) + ... + (n+k-1) = 51
Using the formula for the sum of an arithmetic series, this equation can be rewritten as:
k(2n + k - 1) / 2 = 51
We are also given that the least integer is -50, so we have n = -50. Substituting this value in the equation we have:
k(-99 + k) = 102

Now we have a quadratic equation. We can solve it using the quadratic formula, or notice that the equation can be rewritten as:
(k-51)^2 - 99^2 = 0
This is a difference of squares, so we can factor it as:
(k-51+99)(k-51-99) = 0
The only positive solution is k-51+99 = 0, which gives k = 52.

Answer: Answer("None of the Above") 

(Note: The answer is not among the provided choices. The calculation indicates that the answer is k=52.)
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  We can use the formula for the sum of an arithmetic sequence: sum = (n/2)(2a + (n-1)d)
  Where n is the number of terms in the sequence, a is the first term, and d is the common difference between the terms.
  In this case, we know that the sum is 51, the first term is -50, and we want to find k, the number of terms.
Action: 
  We can write out the sum of the first k consecutive integers starting from -50 as:
  -50 + (-49) + (-48) + ... + (k-2) + (k-1)
  By the formula for the sum of an arithmetic sequence, we have:
  51 = (k/2)((-50) + (k-1))
  Simplifying, we get:
  102 = k(1-k)
  We can rewrite this as a quadratic equation:
  k^2 - k - 102 = 0
  Factoring, we get:
  (k-11)(k+10) = 0
  Since k must be positive, the only possible value is:
  k = 11
  Therefore, the answer is A: 40.
Response 2:
Knowledge:
  - Consecutive integers are integers that follow each other in sequence.
  - The sum of k consecutive integers starting from n is k(n + (n + k - 1)) / 2.
  
Action: 
  - Let's first find out what is the value of the greatest integer.
    - We know that the least integer is -50.
    - Let x be the value of the greatest integer.
    - The k consecutive integers would therefore be -50, -49, -48, ..., x–1, x.
    - Their sum is 51, which means that: k(-50 + x) / 2 = 51
    - We can simplify the equation to k(x-49) = 102
    - Since x is the largest integer of the sequence, it must be larger than or equal to 1 (because -50 + x - 1 = x - 51 is the smallest possible sum of k integers if the largest is x). 
    - Therefore, the only possible values of k are 102/53 or 102/55. Not both of these values result in an integer value of k.
  - Since neither 102/53 nor 102/55 is an integer, none of the given options are correct.
  
Answer: None of the Above.

  In this question, we are given the sum and the first term.

  We can solve for k using this formula.

  a = -50

  k = 3 + 1 = 4

The sum of k consecutive integers that start with n is equal to k * n + (k*(k-1))/2.

Multiplying both sides by 2 to get rid of the fraction, we get:

102 = -100k + k^2 - k

k = (1 ± 201) / (-200)

k = -200 / 202
k ≈ -0.99

  4. Addition and Subtraction (from left to right)

Question: A certain liquid passes through a drain at a rate of w/25 gallons every x seconds. At that rate, how many minutes will it take y gallons to pass through the drain?
Choices:
  A: y/(1200xy)
  B: 20xy/w
  C: 5xy/(12w)
  D: w/(3xy)
  E: 3y/(wx)
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - We can use the unitary method to solve the problem. 
  - The rate of liquid flow is w/25 gallons every x seconds. We can simplify this to w/(25x) gallons per second.
  - The time it takes for y gallons to pass through the drain can be represented as t in minutes.
  - We need to convert the rate from gallons per second to gallons per minute and plug in the values to get an equation to solve for t.

Calculation:
  - The rate in gallons per minute is (w/25) * 60/x = 12w/5x
  - From the formula distance = rate x time, we can derive the following equation in order to solve for t:
      y = (12w/5x)t
  - Solving for t: t = y/(12w/5x) = 5xy/(12w)

Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:

  - To calculate the time it takes for y gallons to pass through the drain, we need to use the formula: time = amount/rate

  - w/25 gallons per x seconds * 60 seconds/1 minutes * 1/1 gallons = 2400w/25x gallons per minute = 96w/xy gallons per minute

Now we can use the formula: time = amount/rate
  - time = y/(96w/xy) = y * xy/96w minutes

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 60 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth?
Choices:
  A: 56
  B: 58
  C: 60
  D: 62
  E: 64
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  If the rectangular piece has dimensions x and y, then we know x * (y - 4) = 2 * 70 since the area of each triangle is 70 and there are two triangles.
  If the original square piece of cloth had side length a, then we know a^2 = x*y by definition.
  We can solve for a in terms of x to get a = sqrt(x*(y+4)).

Action: We want to find the perimeter of the original piece of cloth, which is 4 * a. We already have a in terms of x, so we want to find x and then substitute in to find 4 * a.
Using the first equation, we get:

x * (y - 4) = 2 * 70
x * y - 4x = 140
a^2 - 4x = 140  (substitute x*y with a^2)
a^2 = 4x + 140
a^2 = 4(x + 35)

Since a^2 = (sqrt(x*(y+4)))^2 = x*(y+4), we know:

x * (y + 4) = 4(x + 35)
xy + 4x = 4x + 140
xy = 140

Now we can use xy = 140 to solve for y in terms of x:

y = 140 / x

Substituting for y in a^2 = x*(y+4):

a^2 = x*(140 / x + 4)
a^2 = 140 + 4x
a^2 - 4x = 140

This is the same as the equation we derived earlier, so we know that a^2 = 4(x + 35), and therefore:

a = sqrt(4(x + 35)) = 2 * sqrt(x + 35)

Finally, the perimeter is:

4 * a = 8 * sqrt(x + 35)

We want to find the answer in terms of integers, so we need to find the value of x that makes sqrt(x+35) an integer. Since sqrt(70) = sqrt(2*5*7) is not an integer, we can try the next highest perfect square, which is 9. That means x+35 = 9^2 = 81, so x = 46. Therefore:

perimeter = 8 * sqrt(46 + 35) = 8 * sqrt(81) = 8 * 9 = 72

Answer: Action: Answer("None of the above") 

Since "None of the above" is not an option, the best answer is D: 62. However, this is not correct based on the calculations. The correct answer is not provided in the available choices.

  The square cloth has the same length on all sides.

  The two triangles are congruent, so they have the same area.
  The area of a triangle is given by the formula 1/2*base*height.
  The base and height of each triangle are the sides of the rectangular piece of cloth.
  By the Pythagorean theorem, the length of the diagonal of the rectangular piece is sqrt(2*s^2 - 16s + 16) feet.
  The perimeter of the original square is 4s feet.

  If the area of each triangle is 70 square feet, then 1/2*s*(s-4) = 70.
  Simplifying the equation yields: s^2 - 4s -280 = 0.

  Therefore, the perimeter of the original square is 4*(14 + 4*sqrt(11)) = 56 + 16*sqrt(11)

Response 2:
Knowledge: 
  - The area of each triangle is 70 square feet.
  - The area of a triangle is (1/2) * b * h. Where b is the base of the triangle, and h is the height of the triangle.
  - A square has four equal sides. 
  - The perimeter (P) of a square can be obtained by multiplying the length of one side (s) with 4. That is P = 4s.
  - The rectangular piece obtained after trimming the square cloth will have one side 4 feet less than the other.
  - The diagonally cut rectangle will create two triangles with different base and height but the same area.
  
Approach:
  - Let x be the side of the original square piece of cloth.
  - The rectangular piece obtained after trimming the square cloth has one side x-4.
  - The area of one of the triangle is (1/2) * b * h = 70 sq ft. Since both triangles are equal in area, so their bases and heights are also equal.
  - Therefore, (1/2)(x-4)h = 70, let us simplify this equation.
        (x-4) * h = 140         (1)
  - Since the rectangular piece is diagonally cut in half, the two triangles created will be right-angled triangles.
  - Using Pythagoras' theorem we can write:
        h^2 + (x-4)^2 = x^2     (2)
  - Equation (2) is true because one of the sides of each triangle is x, which is also the side of the original square cloth.
  - We can solve equations (1) and (2) simultaneously to find the value of x.
  
Solution:
  - From equation (1), we can write h = 140 / (x-4).
  - Substituting the value of h in equation (2), we get:
        (140 / (x-4))^2 + (x-4)^2 = x^2
  - Expanding this equation, we get:
        x^4 - 16x^3 + 624x^2 - 8960x + 20096 = 0
  - Factoring this equation, we get:
        (x - 28)(x^3 - 12x^2 + 224x - 716) = 0
  - Since x is the side of a square and hence positive, we can ignore the root x=28. 
  - Therefore, we need to solve the cubic equation x^3 - 12x^2 + 224x - 716 = 0.
  - We can use synthetic division or any other method to solve this equation to get x = 20. 
  - Therefore the perimeter of the original piece of square cloth is P = 4s = 4x = 80 feet.

  A = 1/2 times b times h = 1/2 times x times (l-x+4) = 70
- Solving this equation yields:
  x = 10 or x = 14
  (We can discard x = 10 because the hypotenuse would be longer than the perimeter of the square piece of cloth)
- The perimeter of the original piece of square cloth is 4 times x, which is 4 times 14 = 56 feet.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 61 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet?
Choices:
  A: 46
  B: 81
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge: If we let "l" represent the length of the rectangular parking space and "w" represent the width, then we know: 
    - There are 2 painted sides with length "w" and 1 painted side with length "l"
    - The length of the unpainted side is "l"
    - The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, therefore:
        2w + l = 37
    - The length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, therefore:
        l = 9
Action: 
    Substitute l=9 into 2w + l = 37 to solve for w:
        2w + 9 = 37
        2w = 28
        w = 14
    Now that we know l=9 and w=14, we can calculate the area of the parking space:
        A = lw = 9*14 = 126
Answer: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The painted sides of the rectangular parking space are two adjacent sides and the opposite side.
  If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, then the painted sides have a total length of 37 - 9 = 28 feet.
  We need the length and width of the rectangle to find the area.
  We have two equations: 
    2L + W = 28
    LW = A
  where L is the length, W is the width, and A is the area of the rectangular parking space.
Action: We can start by solving the equation 2L + W = 28 for W to get the W in terms of L.  
  2L + W = 28 
  W = 28 - 2L
  Now we can substitute in the equation LW = A
  L(28 - 2L) = A
  28L - 2L^2 = A
  To maximize the area, we can take the derivative of the area equation, set it to 0, and solve for L. 
  dA/dL = 28 - 4L = 0
  L = 7
  We can substitute L = 7 into equation 2L + W = 28 to find W.
  2(7) + W = 28
  W = 14
  Now we can use LW = A to find the area of the rectangular parking space.
  A = 7 * 14 = 98
  Therefore, the area of the parking space is 98 square feet.

9 + p + 2p = 37 

3p = 28 

p = 9.33 (approx.) 

We can now find the width of the rectangle by subtracting the length of the unpainted side (9) from the sum of the painted sides (2p).

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 63 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Hoses A and B spout water at different constant rates, and hose A can fill a certain pool in 8 hours. Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours and the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. How many hours would it have taken hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 15
  C: 12
  D: 6
  E: 3
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  Let's assume that the rate of hose A is X, and the rate of hose B is Y litres/hour. 
  So, the rate of A+B is (X+Y) litres/hour. 
  The formula distance = rate x time can be used to solve the problem.

  Hose A fills the pool in 8 hours, so the rate of A= X = distance/time = 1/8 pool/hour. 
  In the first 2 hours, hose A can fill:  X x 2 = 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool.
  Then, the remaining fraction of the pool that needs to be filled is: 
  1 - 1/4 = 3/4 of the pool.

  For the remaining 3 hours, the combination of hose A and hose B can fill the remaining 3/4 of the pool. So we have:
  (X+Y) x 3 = 3/4, where X = 1/8.
  
  To solve for Y, let's substitute X = 1/8:
  (1/8 + Y) x 3 = 3/4
  (1/8 + Y) = 1/4
  Y = 1/4 - 1/8 = 1/8

  So, the rate of hose B is Y = 1/8  litres/hour, which means that hose B can fill the entire pool alone in:
  distance = rate x time
  1 = (1/8) x time
  time = 8 hours.

Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  If A can fill a pool in 8 hours, then A's time rate for filling the pool is 1 pool/8 hours = 1/8 pool per hour.
  Let B's time rate for filling the pool be "b".
  "Working together", their combined rate is the sum of their individual rates.
  That is, (1/8) + b = 1/x, where "x" is the time it would take both hoses working together to fill the pool.
  After hose A worked for 2 hours, it only had to fill the remaining part of the pool which was 1 - 1/4 = 3/4 full. The two hoses, working together, filled the remaining 3/4 of the pool in 3 hours. 
  That is, (1/8) * 2 + (3/4) * (1/x) = (3/4) ==> 1/4 + (3/4) * (1/x) = 3/4 ==> (3/4) * (1/x) = 1/2 ==> 1/x = 2/(3/4) ==> 1/x = 8/3 ==> x = 3 hours (the time it would take both hoses working together to fill the pool).

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 64 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two numbers are in the ratio 3:5. If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are in the ratio 12:23. The smaller number is?
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 33
  C: 35
  D: 42
  E: 58
Response 0:
Let the numbers be 3x and 5x. 
When 9 is subtracted from each, we get 3x-9 and 5x-9. 
We are told that (3x-9)/(5x-9) = 12/23. 
Cross multiplying gives us 69x = 207, meaning x = 3. 
Therefore, the smaller number is 3(3) - 9 = 0. 
Action: Answer("None of the Above") since none of the answer options provided match the calculated answer.
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
To solve this problem, we can use the concept that if two quantities are in the ratio a:b, then we can represent them as ax and bx, where x is some constant, and a and b are the ratio. 

Let the numbers be 3x and 5x. 
If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are 3x - 9 and 5x - 9.
According to the problem, (3x - 9)/(5x - 9) = 12/23.

To solve for x we can cross-multiply and solve for x: 

  23(3x-9) = 12(5x-9)
  
  69x - 207 = 60x - 108
  
  9x = 99
  
  x = 11

Now, we can find the smaller number, which is 3x - 9:

  3x - 9 = 3(11) - 9 = 24

0.4y = 1.2 
y = 3

Question: If one of the roots of the quadratic equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0 is 1.5, then what is the value of m?
Choices:
  A: -23.5
  B: -17.5
  C: -10.5
  D: -16.2
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  A quadratic equation is always of the form ax^2 + bx + c =0, where a, b, and c are constants.
  The sum of the roots of a quadratic equation is -b/a where b and a are the coefficients of x and x^2, respectively, and the product of the roots is c/a.
  If one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5, it means that one of the factors in the factorization of the quadratic equation is (x-1.5).
  
Solution:
  Using the factorization of the quadratic equation, we have (x-1.5)(x+a)=0, where a is the value of m.
  Expanding this expression gives x^2 + (a-1.5)x -1.5a = 0.
  Comparing this equation with the given equation we have x^2 + mx + 22 = 0,
  we get a-1.5 = m and -1.5a = 22.
  Solving these equations simultaneously gives a = -44/3 and m = a - 1.5 = -44/3 - 3/2 = -77/6.

Action: Answer("E") since none of the given choices is equal to -77/6.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
To solve a quadratic equation in the form of ax^2 + bx +c = 0, we can use the Quadratic Formula  x = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a.
We can substitute the values of a=1, x=1.5, and c=22 into the quadratic formula to get the value of m.

Action:

m = (-x^2 -22) / x
m = (-1.5^2 -22) / 1.5
m = (-2.25- 22) / 1.5
m = -24.25/1.5
m = -16.17

  In this problem, a = 1, b = m, c = 22, and one root is given as 1.5.

m = -15.5

  -m = 16.2

Topic: Math
Question: In a large forest, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned during 2001. During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year. If the percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags, what is the total deer population in the forest (assuming no change in population between 2001 and 2002)?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 500
  C: 5000
  D: 6000
  E: 7500
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let N be the total deer population in the forest. 
  In 2001, 300 deer in the population were tagged 
  In 2002, 500 deer were caught and only 20 of them had tags from 2001.
  If the percentage of tagged deer in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percentage of tagged deer in the entire population, then (300/N) = (20/500)

Calculation:
  Cross multiplying (300/N) = (20/500) by 500N gives 500*300 = 20N, which gives N = 7500.

Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  - 300 deer were tagged in 2001.
  - 500 deer were caught in 2002, and only 20 of them were tagged from the previous year.
  - The percentage of tagged deer in the 2002 sample is representative of the percentage of tagged deer in the entire population.
  Let x be the total population of deer in the forest, then
  - 300 tagged deer is x * (tagged deer percentage) = x * (0.01 * tagged deer percentage)
  - 20 tagged deer out of 500 caught in 2002 is 0.04 = (tagged deer percentage) * (2002 deer percentage)
  - 500 deer caught in 2002 is x * (2002 deer percentage)
Action: 
  Using the knowledge above, we can set up two equations:
  x * (0.01 * tagged deer percentage) = 300
  (tagged deer percentage) * (2002 deer percentage) = 0.04
  Solve the first equation for (tagged deer percentage):
  tagged deer percentage = 300 / (0.01 * x)
  Substitute into the second equation and solve for (2002 deer percentage):
  (300 / (0.01 * x)) * (2002 deer percentage) = 0.04
  2002 deer percentage = 0.04 * (0.01 * x) / 300 = 0.00013333 * x
  Now we have:
  tagged deer percentage = 300 / (0.01 * x)
  2002 deer percentage = 0.00013333 * x
  The sum of these two percentages is 1, so we can solve:
  300 / (0.01 * x) + 0.00013333 * x = 1
  30000 + 1.3333 * x = 100 * x
  98.6667 * x = 30000
  x = 3048.97
  The total population of deer in the forest is approximately 3049.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 67 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In an exam, a candidate secured 504 marks of the maximum mark of M. If the maximum mark M is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks. What is the value of M?
Choices:
  A: 278
  B: 2890
  C: 270
  D: 2702
  E: 960
Response 0:
Let's create equations based on the given information.

Let's assume the value of M to be x.
Now, we have two sets of values for marks obtained and maximum marks. We can form two equations to determine the value of x.

Candidate secured 504 out of x marks: 504/x = z

When M is converted to 800 marks, the score is 420: 420/800 =z

We can set the two equations equal as they both evaluate to z.

504/x = 420/800

Multiplying both sides by x:

504 = 420/800 * x

Simplifying:

x = (504*800)/420

x = 960

Therefore, the maximum marks (M) is 960.

Action: Answer("E")

Response 3:
Let us solve the problem using a proportion.

Let the maximum mark be M, and let x be the equivalent mark if the maximum mark is converted to 800 marks. We can set up the proportion:
504/M = 420/x

To solve for M, we can cross-multiply and simplify:
504x = 420M
x = 420M/504
x = 35M/42

We also know that x is equivalent to M converted to 800 marks, so we can set up another proportion:
x/800 = M/1

Solving for M:
x/800 = M/1
M = 800(x)
M = 800(35M/42)
M = 800(5/6)M
M = 4000/3

C: 270 - not close
D: 2702 - not close
E: 960 - not close

Response 4:
Knowledge:
  We can use a proportion to solve the problem. If a candidate scored 504 in M, and if M is rescaled to 800, then the equivalent score will be 420. We can set up the proportion `504/M = 420/800`, and solve for M.
  Cross-multiplying the proportion, we get `504 x 800 = 420 x M`.
  Then, `M = 504 x 800 / 420 = 960`.
    A: 278 is not the correct answer.
    B: 2890 is not the correct answer.
    C: 270 is not the correct answer.
    D: 2702 is not the correct answer.

Let M be the maximum mark.

If the maximum mark M is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks.

This means that the ratio of his new score to the new maximum is equal to the ratio of his old score to the old maximum.

504/M = 420/800

We can simplify the right-hand side of the equation to 21/40:
504/M = 21/40

Cross-multiplying yields:
21M = 20160

Solving for M:
M = 960.

Therefore, the value of M is 960.

Question: On dividing 2272 and 875 by a 3-digit number N, we get the same remainder. The sum of the digits of N is:
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 11
  C: 12
  D: 13
  E: 14
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If a number gives the same remainder when we divide different numbers by it, it must divide the difference of those numbers.
  If a number x divides a and b, then it must divide a-b.
  The sum of the digits of a 3-digit number would be at least 1+0+0 = 1 and at most 9+9+9 = 27.

Let N be the unknown 3-digit number and r be the common remainder.
We know that:
  2272 = N*q + r  for some quotient q
  875 = N*p + r   for some quotient p

Subtracting the two equations above gives:
  1397 = N*(q-p)

The right side of the equation above is divisible by N. Therefore, N must be a divisor of 1397.

1397 is a prime number that cannot be factored into 3-digit numbers. Therefore, N must be 1-digit only.

Checking its remainders when dividing 2272 and 875 by 1397, we can find that both leave a remainder of 978.

Therefore, N = 1397 and the sum of its digits is 1+3+9+7 = 20.
Action: Answer("None of the Above (not a valid choice)") since none of the provided choices is correct.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  When a number X is divided by N, the remainder R must be smaller than N. Thus, N >= R.
  The remainder of a division X/N is the same as the remainder of X-YN for any integer Y.
  If two numbers have the same remainder when divided by N, then their difference also has a remainder of 0 when divided by N.
  If the remainder of the division X/N is R, then X-N, X-2N, X-3N, etc. will all have the same remainder of R when divided by N.
  
To find N:
  Let's assume that the remainder is X. So, according to question:
  2272 - X = aN   ;   875 - X = bN
  where a and b are any integers
  (2272 - X) - 2*(875 - X) = aN - 2bN = (a-2b)N = 2272 - 2*875
  (a-2b)N = 522
  Since N is a three-digit number, the only possible values for N are 1,2,3,6,9,  13, 17, 26, 39, 78, 174, 261, 522. Only 261 satisfies the condition that sum of the digits of N is an integer.
  
To find the sum of digits of N:
  Sum of digits of 261 = 2+6+1 = 9

Question: By himself, Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours. On a particular day, he happens to finish two-thirds of the work. The remaining portion of the work is done by Jill, whose rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do. How long does it take Jill to finish the remaining work?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 8
  C: 22
  D: 50
  E: 20
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  If Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, then he can clean 1/12 th of it per hour.
  If Jack finishes two-thirds of the work, it means remaining one-third part of work is still left.
  Jill's rate of cleaning is 5% of what Jack can do. So, Jill can clean 5/100 th or 1/20th part of work per hour.
  We need to find the time it takes for Jill to clean the remaining one-third part of the yacht, given her work rate.
Solution: 
  If Jack finishes two-thirds of the work, then the remaining one-third of work is left. 
  Jack's rate of work is 1/12th of the yacht per hour. Let the time taken by Jill to clean the remaining one-third part be x.
  Jill's work rate is 1/20 th of the yacht per hour.
  Using the work formula, we get:
  (1/12)*2/3 + (1/20)*x = 1
  2/36 + (1/20)*x = 1
  1/10*x = 1 - 1/18
  x = (8/9) * 10
Action: Answer("B") i.e 8.

  If Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, then his rate of work is 1/12 of a yacht per hour.
  Two-thirds of the job is left to be completed by Jill

  Rate * Time = Work

  Now we can find how long Jill takes to complete the remaining work.
  (2/15)*t = (1/3)
  t = (1/3) / (2/15) = 7.5

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 70 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Mr.Sam takes 17 hours to go by train to a certain city and return by car. He loses 4 hours if he goes both ways by train. How long would he have taken if he had traveled by car in both ways?
Choices:
  A: 22 hrs
  B: 18 hrs
  C: 16 hrs
  D: 20 hrs
  E: 13 hrs
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let d be the distance between the two cities.
  Let s be the speed of the train and let the speed of the car be c.
  We know that time = distance / speed.

Solution:
  Going by train to the city takes Mr. Sam 17 hrs. That is:
  17 = d/s.

  Traveling back from the city to his starting point by car takes Mr. Sam x hours. That is:
  x = d/c.

  If he goes both ways by train, he loses 4 hours. So, he will have traveled for a total of 17*2 - 4 = 30 hours.

  We can add the time taken for both legs of the journey to find that the distance d is:
  17s + x = 30
  Substituting x = d/c, we get:
  17s + d/c = 30

  We are asked to find how long he would have taken if he had traveled by car in both ways. This means his total time would be:
  2x = 2d/c

  We need to find d to solve x. We can do this by isolating "d" from the second equation above:
  d = (30c - 17s)c/(2c)

  Plugging this into the first equation to solve for s:
  17 = [(30c - 17s)c/(2c)] /s
  17 = (30c - 17s) / (2s)

  Solving for s, we end up with s = (30c - 17s)/(34).
  We are interested in finding x = d/c. We can substitute d in terms of s to get:
  x = d/c = (30c - 17s)c/(2c^2)

  Simplifying, we get:
  x = (30c - 17[(30c - 17s)/(34)]) / 2c = (51s) / (34c)

  The time taken if he had traveled by car in both ways would be 2x:
  2x = 2[(51s) / (34c)] = (51s) / (17c) = (51/17)(d/c)
  but d = 17s
  so we have
  2x = (51/17)(17s/c) = 3s.

  Therefore, the time he would have taken if he had traveled by car in both ways is 3 * 17 = 51 hours.

Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
The time taken for the train journey to the city combined with the time taken for the journey back by car = 17 hours.
The time taken for the train journey to the city combined with the time taken for the journey back by train = 21 hours (17 hours + 4 hours lost).
We can represent,
Time taken for the train journey to the city = x
Time taken for the journey back by car = 17 - x
Time taken for the journey back by train = 21 - x

Their sum gives 17:  x + (17 - x) = 17
                          x = 8.5

Therefore, the time Mr.Sam took for the journey back by car = 17 - 8.5 - 4 = 4.5.
So, the total time taken to travel by car in both ways = 2 * 4.5 hours = 9 hours.

Question: For bringing each copper coin from the bottom of a river, a coin-diver gets 20 cents, and for each brass coin she gets 25 cents. If after one dive, she got $3.40. What is the minimum number of copper coins that she brought?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 3
  C: 2
  D: 1
  E: 0
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let c be the number of copper coins and b be the number of brass coins.
  For each copper coin, the coin-diver gets $0.20
  For each brass coin, the coin-diver gets $0.25
  After one dive, the coin-diver got a total of $3.40

Action: 
  Let's use algebra: 
  c -> number of copper coins
  b -> number of brass coins
  Total earned from copper coins = 0.20c
  Total earned from brass coins = 0.25b
  Total earned from both = 0.20c + 0.25b
  Given, 0.20c + 0.25b = 3.40
  Multiplying both sides by 100, we get 20c + 25b = 340
  Taking the first equation (Total earned from copper coins) and subtracting it from the previous equation, we get:
  5b = 340 - 20c
  5b = 5(68 - 4c)
  b = 68 - 4c
  Since b and c are both non-negative integers and b must be at least 1, we can find the minimum value of c by finding the largest possible value of b:
  b = 1, c = (68 - 4) = 64
  So, the coin-diver brought a minimum of 64 copper coins.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 10.0 | Problem 72 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17, and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order. Find the number.
Choices:
  A: 368
  B: 377
  C: 288
  D: 997
  E: 112
Response 0:
Let the three digit number be represented by (100a + 10b + c).
We know that a+b+c = 17 (1) and a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109 (2).
If (100a + 10b + c) - 495 = 100c + 10b + a. Then, 99a - 99c = 495, which simplifies as a - c = 5 (3).
Squaring equation (1), we get a^2 + b^2 + c^2 + 2(ab+ac+bc) = 289 (4).
Adding equations (2) and (4), and using equation (3), we get 2(a^2 + b^2 +c^2) + 10(ab+bc) = 389 (5).
Substituting equation (2) in equation (5), and simplifying, we get ab+bc = 10 (6).
From equation (1), we can write b = (17 - a - c).
Substituting that in equation (6), we get ac + c^2 - 7c = 0.
Solving the above quadratic equation, we get c = 7 or c = 1.
If c = 7, then a+b = 10.
Also, from equation (3), a-c = 5, which is not possible if a and c are both odd or both even. Hence, c = 1.
If c = 1, then a+b = 16.
Substituting c = 1 in equation (2), we get a^2 + b^2 + 1 = 109, which simplifies as a^2 + b^2 = 108.
We can solve this equation using trial and error (for instance, a=3 and b=9). 
Therefore, the number is 319.
Now, check that 319 - 495 = 913, which consists of the same digits as 319 written in reverse order.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Let's call the hundreds digit "A", the tens digit "B", and the units digit "C".
We know that A + B + C = 17, and A^2 + B^2 + C^2 = 109.
From the third sentence, we know that the number is a palindrome (a number that reads the same forward and backward) after subtracting 495. 
Let's create an equation with that information:
100A + 10B + C - 495 = 100C + 10B + A
99A - 99C = 495
A - C = 5

Now we have two equations with two variables. We can use the first equation to solve for one variable in terms of the other.
A + B + C = 17
C = 17 - A - B

Substituting that expression into the second equation and simplifying, we find that:
A^2 + B^2 + (17 - A - B)^2 = 109
2A^2 + 2B^2 - 34A - 34B + 170 = 0
A^2 + B^2 - 17A - 17B + 85 = 0

The question asks for a three-digit number, so A cannot be 0 or 1. We can now look at the answer choices:
A) 368: A = 3, B = 6, C = 8. This doesn't work because A - C ≠ 5.
B) 377: A = 3, B = 7, C = 7. This works!
C) 288: A = 2, B = 8, C = 8. This doesn't work because A - C ≠ 5.
D) 997: A = 9, B = 9, C = 7. This doesn't work because the sum of the digits is 25, not 17.
E) 112: A = 1, B = 1, C = 2. This doesn't work because A - C ≠ 5.

Therefore, the answer is B) 377.

100x + 10y + z - 495 = 100z + 10y + x

Response 5:
Let the three digit number be abc so that:
a + b + c = 17 ...(1)
a² + b² + c² = 109 ...(2)

When 495 is subtracted from the number, the resulting number backwards is cba. So we can write:
100a + 10b + c - 495 = 100c + 10b + a
99a - 99c = 495
a - c = 5 ...(3)

We can solve equations (1) and (3) simultaneously to get a and c:
a + b + c = 17 ...(1)
a - c = 5  ...(3)

c = 6 and a = 11 - b

2b² - 12b + 48 = 0

b = 3 ± √3

We select the positive root b = 3 + √3, since the sum of digits is 17, abc must be equal to:
110 + √3

Finally, we confirm that this number satisfies all the original conditions:
1 + 1 + 3 + √3 = 6 + √3, which satisfies equation (1)
1² + 1² + (3 + √3)² = 1 + 1 + 9 + 6√3 + 3 = 14 + 6√3, which satisfies equation (2)
(110 + √3) - 495 = 604 - 110 - √3 = 394 - √3
We can now reverse the digits of 394 - √3 to get 3 + √3
So the answer is the number abc = 110 + √3, which is closest to 112.

a + b + c = 17
a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109
When we subtract 495 from the number, we get the number def, where:
def = 100c + 10b + a - 495 = 100a + 10b + c

99a - 90c = 495
11a - 10c = 55
Now we can use the first equation to eliminate c:
c = 17 - a - b
Substituting into the second equation, we get:
a^2 + b^2 + (17-a-b)^2 = 109
2a^2 + 2b^2 - 34a - 34b + 242 = 109

a^2 + b^2 - 17a - 17b + 66 = 0
(a-8)^2 + (b-9)^2 = 5^2
The only two-digit numbers that differ by 1 and have squares that add up to 25 are 3 and 4. Therefore, a can only be 3 or 13; but if a = 13, then b would be negative, so we must have a = 3 and b = 4. Then we can solve for c:
3 + 4 + c = 17
c = 10
Therefore, abc = 344, and def = 443.

We are given that the sum of the digits of a three-digit number is 17 and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. Therefore, we can write:

x + y + z = 17
x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = 109

Now, let's carry out the subtraction: " If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order."

Subtracting 495 from the original number will give us a new three-digit number "abc" where a, b, and c are digits representing the same digits as the original number, but written in reverse order. We can thus write:
xyz - 495 = abc
100x + 10y + z - 495 = 100a + 10b + c
100x - 100a + 10y - 10b + z - c = 495
Dividing through by 10, we have:
10x - 10a + y - b + (z - c)/10 = 49.5
or
10x - 10a + y - b = 49        (since z and c must be the same, and (z-c)/10=0)

We now have a system of three equations:
x+ y + z = 17 (1)
x^2+ y^2+ z^2 = 109 (2)
10x - 10a + y - b = 49 (3)

We can use Equation (1) to solve for z in terms of x and y:
z = 17 - x - y

We can then substitute this into Equation (2) and simplify to get:
x^2 + y^2 + (17 - x - y)^2 = 109
2x^2 + 2y^2 - 34x - 34y + 138 = 0
Dividing by 2, we get:
x^2 + y^2 - 17x - 17y + 69 = 0  (4)

Next, we can use Equation (3) to solve for b in terms of x, y, and a:
b = 10x - 10a - y + 49

We can then substitute this into Equation (4) to get a quadratic equation in terms of x and y:
x^2 + y^2 - 17x - 17y + 69 = 0
x^2 + (10x - 10a - y + 49)^2 - 17x - 17(10x - 10a - y + 49) + 69 = 0
101x^2 - 2060x + 10100a - 4010y + 1989 = 0

We can simplify this by using Equation (1) to solve for a in terms of x and y:
a = 17 - x - y

Substituting this in, we get:
101x^2 - 2060x + 10100(17-x-y) - 4010y + 1989 = 0
101x^2 - 2060x - 10100x - 4010y + 10100y + 183289 = 0
101x^2 - 13160x + 183289 = 0

We can now use the quadratic formula to solve for x:
x = (13160 ± sqrt(13160^2 - 4(101)(183289))) / 2(101)

After simplification, this gives us two values for x: x = 8 and x = 5.

We can then use Equation (1) to solve for y and z for each value of x:

If x = 8:
y + z = 9        (from Equation (1))
y^2 + z^2 = 45   (from Equation (2))
10(8) - 10a + y - b = 49      (from Equation (3))
